9-32 DECKLISTS
==============



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on February 28, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/calderaro.jpg)
By Marc Calderaro











Top 8 decklists just aren’t enough, are they? Well luckily, we’ve got your back. Here are the decks that came in 9th through 32nd place at Grand Prix Houston. Enjoy!




---
